# I-run11-007 (#1051) diff review — pin every LLM role to stable+fast OpenRouter providers with ranked fallback

## Context (root cause, evidence-backed)
The drb_72 runs 14/15/16 Mirror "blanks" are NOT the model: GLM-5.1 emits clean cited answers in the production config (reasoning ON, 16384 tokens) on every provider tested (Phala/Together/Chutes/Fireworks/Baidu/DeepInfra — all non-blank). The blanks are INTERMITTENT provider failures. The OpenRouter provider-routing docs confirm allow_fallbacks does NOT fire on an empty 200 (finish=stop, 0 tokens) — only on error-class outcomes — so a provider that returns empty hands us a blank with no auto-advance. Our verifier transport set only {require_parameters:True} with no provider order/ignore/fallback.

## What the diff does
1. config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml (generated by scripts/diagnostics/rank_openrouter_providers.py from LIVE endpoint health: status==0 + uptime_last_30m>=98 gate, sort throughput p50 desc / latency p50 asc, emit provider SLUGS from tag-prefix, dedup per provider). Per role: order (ranked healthy) + ignore (flaky excluded, e.g. Mirror's phala/together).
2. src/polaris_graph/roles/provider_routing.py (NEW): loads the config, apply_provider_routing merges order+ignore+allow_fallbacks:False into the provider block. Degrades gracefully (PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING=0 or absent role -> None -> prior behavior).
3. openrouter_role_transport._build_openrouter_body: pins BOTH the reasoning and non-reasoning role provider blocks. complete() empty-retry: on BlankVerdictError, adds the served provider to provider.ignore so the retry advances to the next healthy provider; a ROUTED non-reasoning role gets (1+PG_PROVIDER_BLANK_RETRIES) attempts (single attempt preserved when unrouted -> the classifier-single-attempt invariant holds with routing OFF).
4. openrouter_client (generator): config-driven order+ignore+allow_fallbacks:False when no env/Path-B override (env still wins).
5. tests: tests/roles + tests/dr_benchmark conftest default routing OFF (assert base block); test_provider_routing.py covers loader + block-build + the empty-response provider-exclusion retry against a deterministic fixture. 652 role+benchmark tests green.

## Verify especially (Red-Team)
- allow_fallbacks:False + order semantics: does this correctly restrict to the listed healthy providers AND never route to an unlisted flaky one? Is dropping the empty-fallback to OUR retry correct given OpenRouter won't auto-advance on empty?
- The empty-retry: served `provider` is the DISPLAY name; is adding it to `ignore` (which the order list uses SLUGS) reliable? (We verified OpenRouter accepts display names in `order`; confirm `ignore` semantics.) Any risk the retry loops on the same provider or never converges? Budget-cap accounting on each blank attempt still holds?
- The non-reasoning ladder gating on role_is_routed: any role where this regresses the prior single-attempt or the reasoning step-down ladder?
- Family-distinctness / served==pinned (M4) unaffected by provider routing? (provider changes the SERVER, not the model family.)
- Sovereignty: OpenRouter is already the benchmark/dev path (US router) — provider routing here does not change the sovereign self-host destination. OK?
- LAW VI no-hardcode: order/ignore come from config, regenerated from live health. OK?

## Output schema (REQUIRED)
verdict: APPROVE | REQUEST_CHANGES
novel_p0: [...]
continuing_p0: [...]
p1: [...]
p2: [...]
convergence_call: continue | accept_remaining
remaining_blockers_for_execution: [...]

```diff
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""I-run11-005 PHASE-4 reproduction: does GLM-5.1 Mirror blank at MAX reasoning on HARD claims, and
+does a bigger token budget fix it? Hypothesis (from mirror_production_config_test: GLM used 12210 of
+16384 reasoning tokens on a SIMPLE claim): on a HARD multi-part claim, xhigh reasoning consumes the
+whole budget → no room for the verdict → BlankVerdictError. If true, the runs-14/15/16 blanks are
+token-budget starvation (a config/seam fix: raise PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS), NOT the model.
+
+Goes through the REAL complete() path (incl. the blank-recovery ladder), so the captured result is
+the END state the seam would see. Sweeps the budget per claim. Reads OPENROUTER_API_KEY from .env
+(never printed). Run from repo root. ~8 live calls.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+import os, sys, json
+
+os.environ.pop("PG_MIRROR_REASONING", None)   # production default: reasoning ON for mirror
+os.environ["PG_MIRROR_MODEL"] = "z-ai/glm-5.1"
+os.environ.setdefault("PG_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT", "openrouter")
+if not os.getenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY"):
+    try:
+        for line in open(".env", encoding="utf-8"):
+            if line.startswith("OPENROUTER_API_KEY="):
+                os.environ["OPENROUTER_API_KEY"] = line.split("=", 1)[1].strip().strip('"').strip("'")
+                break
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+sys.path.insert(0, ".")
+import httpx  # noqa: E402
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.openrouter_role_transport import OpenRouterRoleTransport  # noqa: E402
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.mirror_adapter import build_mirror_pass1_request  # noqa: E402
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.role_transport import EvidenceDocument  # noqa: E402
+
+# a SIMPLE control + HARD multi-part claims (force lots of grounding reasoning across many docs)
+CLAIMS = {
+    "simple": "Automation can displace workers from specific tasks.",
+    "hard_multipart": (
+        "Across these studies automation simultaneously displaced workers from routine tasks, "
+        "depressed relative wages for the middle of the skill distribution, complemented high-skill "
+        "labor, and—alongside generative-AI assistance that raised customer-support productivity "
+        "by about 15% concentrated among less-experienced agents—netted out to no collapse in "
+        "aggregate labor demand over the period studied."
+    ),
+    "hard_numeric": (
+        "Industrial-robot adoption reduced both employment and wages in local US labor markets, with "
+        "each additional robot per thousand workers lowering the employment-to-population ratio and "
+        "average wages by a quantified amount, even after accounting for complementary task creation."
+    ),
+}
+
+
+def docs():
+    e = json.load(open("outputs/audits/I-run11-004/m25_bakeoff/evidence_pool.json", encoding="utf-8"))
+    out = []
+    for x in e:
+        q = x.get("direct_quote") or ""
+        if len(q) > 200 and x.get("evidence_id"):
+            out.append(EvidenceDocument(doc_id=x["evidence_id"], text=q))
+        if len(out) >= 5:
+            break
+    return out
+
+
+def run(claim_label: str, claim: str, budget: int, ev):
+    os.environ["PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS"] = str(budget)
+    req = build_mirror_pass1_request(claim, ev, model_slug="z-ai/glm-5.1")
+    transport = OpenRouterRoleTransport(httpx.Client(timeout=300.0))
+    try:
+        resp = transport.complete(req)
+        raw = resp.raw_text or ""
+        rlen = len(getattr(resp, "reasoning", None) or "")
+        print(f"  [{claim_label} @ budget={budget}] content={len(raw)} reasoning={rlen} "
+              f"has_<co>={'<co' in raw} blank={len(raw.strip()) == 0}")
+    except Exception as ex:  # noqa: BLE001 — diagnostic
+        print(f"  [{claim_label} @ budget={budget}] {type(ex).__name__}: {str(ex)[:120]}")
+
+
+def main():
+    ev = docs()
+    print(f"payload {len(ev)} docs; GLM-5.1 reasoning ON (xhigh); sweeping budget\n")
+    for label, claim in CLAIMS.items():
+        for budget in (16384, 40000):
+            run(label, claim, budget, ev)
+        print()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""DEFINITIVE model-vs-config test (I-run11-005): reproduce the EXACT production Mirror config that
+blanked in runs 14/15 — reasoning ON (the _ROLE_REASONING_DEFAULT mirror=True default, which
+run_gate_b.py does NOT override) + PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS=16384 (default) + a realistic
+multi-document payload. My earlier bakeoff/pre-merge tests all ran reasoning-OFF at 4000 tokens — a
+DIFFERENT config — so they never exercised what actually failed.
+
+Captures raw_text + reasoning length + blank status, for GLM-5.1 and nemotron, reasoning ON. If GLM
+blanks here (adequate 16k budget) while nemotron emits, the blank is GLM's reasoning-first exhaustion
+(model). If GLM also emits, the production blank had another (seam/transient) cause. Honest either way.
+
+Reads OPENROUTER_API_KEY from env/.env (never printed). Run from repo root. ~4-6 live calls.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+import os, sys, json
+
+# PRODUCTION config: do NOT set PG_MIRROR_REASONING (defaults to True for mirror) and do NOT lower
+# the reasoning token budget (defaults to 16384) — exactly what run_gate_b.py uses.
+os.environ.pop("PG_MIRROR_REASONING", None)
+os.environ.pop("PG_SENTINEL_MAX_TOKENS", None)
+os.environ.setdefault("PG_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT", "openrouter")
+if not os.getenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY"):
+    try:
+        for line in open(".env", encoding="utf-8"):
+            if line.startswith("OPENROUTER_API_KEY="):
+                os.environ["OPENROUTER_API_KEY"] = line.split("=", 1)[1].strip().strip('"').strip("'")
+                break
+    except Exception:
+        pass
+
+sys.path.insert(0, ".")
+import httpx  # noqa: E402
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.openrouter_role_transport import (  # noqa: E402
+    OpenRouterRoleTransport, role_reasoning_enabled,
+)
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.mirror_adapter import build_mirror_pass1_request  # noqa: E402
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.role_transport import EvidenceDocument  # noqa: E402
+
+CLAIM = ("Automation has historically displaced workers from specific tasks while complementary "
+         "forces and new task creation kept aggregate labor demand from collapsing.")
+
+
+def realistic_docs():
+    e = json.load(open("outputs/audits/I-run11-004/m25_bakeoff/evidence_pool.json", encoding="utf-8"))
+    # a realistic seam payload: several FULL evidence docs (not truncated to 2000), like production
+    docs = []
+    for x in e:
+        q = x.get("direct_quote") or ""
+        if len(q) > 200 and x.get("evidence_id"):
+            docs.append(EvidenceDocument(doc_id=x["evidence_id"], text=q))
+        if len(docs) >= 5:
+            break
+    return docs
+
+
+def run_one(slug: str, docs):
+    os.environ["PG_MIRROR_MODEL"] = slug
+    reasoning = role_reasoning_enabled("mirror", slug)  # confirm production default
+    req = build_mirror_pass1_request(CLAIM, docs, model_slug=slug)
+    transport = OpenRouterRoleTransport(httpx.Client(timeout=300.0))
+    try:
+        resp = transport.complete(req)
+        raw = resp.raw_text or ""
+        reasoning_txt = getattr(resp, "reasoning", None) or ""
+        print(f"[{slug}] reasoning_enabled={reasoning} served={resp.served_model}")
+        print(f"    content_len={len(raw)} reasoning_len={len(reasoning_txt)} "
+              f"has_<co>={'<co' in raw} blank={len(raw.strip()) == 0}")
+        print(f"    raw_text[:300]={raw[:300]!r}")
+    except Exception as ex:  # noqa: BLE001 — diagnostic: surface the failure verbatim
+        print(f"[{slug}] reasoning_enabled={reasoning} EXC {type(ex).__name__}: {str(ex)[:180]}")
+
+
+def main():
+    docs = realistic_docs()
+    total = sum(len(d.text) for d in docs)
+    print(f"payload: {len(docs)} full docs, {total} chars (realistic seam size)\n")
+    for slug in ["z-ai/glm-5.1", "nvidia/nemotron-3-super-120b-a12b"]:
+        run_one(slug, docs)
+        print()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""I-run11-005 root-cause confirm: is the Mirror blank an OpenRouter PROVIDER-routing issue, not the
+model? GLM-5.1 has 19 providers (2 degraded: Phala status -5/49% uptime, Together -2/83%). Our
+transport does NOT restrict the provider, so a Mirror call can land on a flaky one that returns empty
+content (finish_reason:error, 0 tokens) -> BlankVerdictError. This forces GLM onto specific providers
+(allow_fallbacks=false) on the SAME hard claim + realistic payload + reasoning ON, and reports which
+return empty. If the degraded providers blank and the healthy ones don't, provider routing is the
+cause and the fix is provider preferences (exclude flaky / fallback-on-empty), NOT a model swap.
+
+Reads OPENROUTER_API_KEY from .env (never printed). Run from repo root. ~6 live calls.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+import json, os, sys, urllib.request, urllib.error
+
+key = os.getenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
+if not key:
+    for line in open(".env", encoding="utf-8"):
+        if line.startswith("OPENROUTER_API_KEY="):
+            key = line.split("=", 1)[1].strip().strip('"').strip("'"); break
+
+e = json.load(open("outputs/audits/I-run11-004/m25_bakeoff/evidence_pool.json", encoding="utf-8"))
+docs = [(x["evidence_id"], x["direct_quote"]) for x in e
+        if len(x.get("direct_quote") or "") > 200 and x.get("evidence_id")][:5]
+DOC_BLOCK = "\n\n".join(f"[doc {i}: {d}]\n{q[:2000]}" for i, (d, q) in enumerate(docs))
+CLAIM = ("Across these studies automation displaced workers from routine tasks, depressed relative "
+         "wages for the middle of the skill distribution, complemented high-skill labor, and netted "
+         "out to no collapse in aggregate labor demand over the period studied.")
+PROMPT = (f"Documents:\n{DOC_BLOCK}\n\nClaim:\n{CLAIM}\n\nQuote the exact supporting spans from the "
+          "documents using <co>covered text</co:doc_id> citation tags, then judge the claim.")
+
+# degraded providers first, then a healthy control set
+PROVIDERS = ["Phala", "Together", "Chutes", "Fireworks", "Baidu", "DeepInfra"]
+
+
+def call(provider: str) -> str:
+    body = {
+        "model": "z-ai/glm-5.1",
+        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": PROMPT}],
+        "max_tokens": 16384,
+        "reasoning": {"enabled": True, "effort": "high"},
+        "provider": {"order": [provider], "allow_fallbacks": False},
+    }
+    req = urllib.request.Request(
+        "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions",
+        data=json.dumps(body).encode(),
+        headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}", "Content-Type": "application/json"},
+    )
+    try:
+        r = json.loads(urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=90).read())
+    except urllib.error.HTTPError as ex:
+        return f"HTTP {ex.code}: {ex.read()[:140].decode(errors='ignore')}"
+    except Exception as ex:  # noqa: BLE001
+        return f"{type(ex).__name__}: {str(ex)[:120]}"
+    ch = (r.get("choices") or [{}])[0]
+    msg = ch.get("message", {}) or {}
+    content = (msg.get("content") or "")
+    reasoning = (msg.get("reasoning") or "")
+    served = (r.get("provider") or "?")
+    fr = ch.get("finish_reason")
+    err = r.get("error")
+    return (f"served={served} content_len={len(content)} reasoning_len={len(reasoning)} "
+            f"finish={fr} blank={len(content.strip()) == 0}" + (f" ERROR={err}" if err else ""))
+
+
+def main():
+    print("forcing GLM-5.1 onto each provider (allow_fallbacks=False), hard claim, reasoning ON\n",
+          flush=True)
+    for p in PROVIDERS:
+        print(f"[{p:10}] {call(p)}", flush=True)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""I-run11-007 (#1051): rank each role model's OpenRouter providers by STABILITY + SPEED and emit
+config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml — the ranked, healthy-only provider order used to
+pin every LLM to a stable+fast provider with a deterministic fallback chain that NEVER routes to a
+broken server.
+
+Ranking (per the research on /docs provider-selection): keep only operational endpoints
+(status==0), then sort by uptime_last_30m desc, latency_last_30m asc, throughput_last_30m desc.
+The `order` list is the ranked healthy chain (used with allow_fallbacks:false so off-list flaky
+providers are never tried). The `ignore` list is the explicit deny-list of broken endpoints
+(status!=0 or uptime below the floor) as belt-and-suspenders.
+
+Reads OPENROUTER_API_KEY from env/.env (never printed). Deterministic given live data. Run from repo root.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+import json, os, sys, urllib.request
+
+UPTIME_FLOOR = float(os.getenv("PG_PROVIDER_UPTIME_FLOOR", "98.0"))
+TOP_N = int(os.getenv("PG_PROVIDER_ORDER_TOP_N", "6"))
+ROLE_MODELS = {
+    "generator": "deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro",
+    "mirror": "z-ai/glm-5.1",
+    "sentinel": "minimax/minimax-m2",
+    "judge": "qwen/qwen3.6-35b-a3b",
+}
+
+key = os.getenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
+if not key:
+    for line in open(".env", encoding="utf-8"):
+        if line.startswith("OPENROUTER_API_KEY="):
+            key = line.split("=", 1)[1].strip().strip('"').strip("'"); break
+if not key:
+    print("NO OPENROUTER_API_KEY"); sys.exit(2)
+
+
+def endpoints(model: str) -> list[dict]:
+    req = urllib.request.Request(
+        f"https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models/{model}/endpoints",
+        headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"},
+    )
+    return json.loads(urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=30).read())["data"].get("endpoints", [])
+
+
+def rank(eps: list[dict]) -> tuple[list[str], list[str], list[str]]:
+    healthy, broken = [], []
+    for e in eps:
+        up = e.get("uptime_last_30m")
+        operational = e.get("status") == 0 and (up is None or up >= UPTIME_FLOOR)
+        (healthy if operational else broken).append(e)
+
+    def p50(v):
+        # latency/throughput are percentile dicts {p50,p75,p90,p99}; a scalar or None is tolerated.
+        if isinstance(v, dict):
+            return v.get("p50")
+        return v
+
+    def sort_key(e: dict):
+        # Stability is already GATED (uptime>=floor + status==0). Among the stable set, rank by SPEED:
+        # throughput p50 desc PRIMARY (our verifier calls are reasoning-heavy = long outputs, so
+        # tokens/sec dominates total time), latency p50 asc secondary (time-to-first-token), uptime
+        # desc final tiebreak. None metrics rank last. -> "stable (gated) AND fastest (sorted)".
+        tput = p50(e.get("throughput_last_30m"))
+        lat = p50(e.get("latency_last_30m"))
+        up = e.get("uptime_last_30m")
+        return (
+            -(tput if tput is not None else -1.0),
+            (lat if lat is not None else float("inf")),
+            -(up if up is not None else -1.0),
+        )
+
+    def slug(e: dict) -> str:
+        # OpenRouter provider.order/ignore expects the provider SLUG (the `tag` prefix before '/',
+        # e.g. 'deepinfra/fp4' -> 'deepinfra'), NOT the display provider_name ('DeepInfra' / 'Io Net').
+        tag = e.get("tag") or ""
+        return tag.split("/")[0] if tag else (e.get("provider_name") or "").lower().replace(" ", "-")
+
+    healthy.sort(key=sort_key)
+
+    def dedup(eps_list: list[dict]) -> list[str]:
+        # a provider may expose several quant endpoints; keep its FIRST (best-ranked) slug only.
+        seen, out = set(), []
+        for e in eps_list:
+            s = slug(e)
+            if s and s not in seen:
+                seen.add(s); out.append(s)
+        return out
+
+    order = dedup(healthy)[:TOP_N]
+    ignore = [s for s in dedup(broken) if s not in set(order)]
+    notes = []
+    if len(healthy) < 3:
+        notes.append(f"THIN POOL: only {len(healthy)} healthy provider(s)")
+    if any(e.get("uptime_last_30m") is None for e in healthy):
+        notes.append("some providers have NULL uptime (ranked last)")
+    return order, ignore, notes
+
+
+def _slug_of(e: dict) -> str:
+    tag = e.get("tag") or ""
+    return tag.split("/")[0] if tag else (e.get("provider_name") or "").lower().replace(" ", "-")
+
+
+def main():
+    out_lines = [
+        "# I-run11-007 (#1051): per-role OpenRouter provider routing — ranked HEALTHY chain.",
+        "# Generated by scripts/diagnostics/rank_openrouter_providers.py from live endpoint health.",
+        f"# Ranking: status==0 + uptime_last_30m>={UPTIME_FLOOR}, sorted uptime desc / latency asc / throughput desc.",
+        "# Used with allow_fallbacks:false so off-list (flaky) providers are NEVER tried.",
+        "# Re-generate before a demo to refresh health. LAW VI: consumed as config, never inlined.",
+        "roles:",
+    ]
+    print(f"floor={UPTIME_FLOOR} top_n={TOP_N}\n")
+    aliases: dict[str, str] = {}  # served display provider_name -> routing slug (for empty-retry exclusion)
+    for role, model in ROLE_MODELS.items():
+        try:
+            eps = endpoints(model)
+        except Exception as ex:  # noqa: BLE001
+            print(f"{role} {model}: FETCH ERROR {str(ex)[:80]}"); continue
+        for e in eps:
+            name = e.get("provider_name")
+            if name:
+                aliases.setdefault(name, _slug_of(e))
+        order, ignore, notes = rank(eps)
+        print(f"{role:10} ({model}): order={order}  ignore={ignore}  {notes}")
+        out_lines += [
+            f"  {role}:",
+            f"    model: {model}",
+            f"    order: [{', '.join(order)}]",
+            f"    ignore: [{', '.join(ignore)}]",
+        ]
+        if notes:
+            out_lines.append(f"    notes: \"{'; '.join(notes)}\"")
+    # provider_aliases: maps the served display `provider` (e.g. 'AtlasCloud', 'Io Net') back to the
+    # routing slug ('atlas-cloud', 'io-net') so the empty-retry excludes the SAME identity that
+    # `provider.ignore`/`order` use (Codex diff-gate iter-1 P1 — a naive lower/space-fold mis-maps
+    # camelCase providers like AtlasCloud -> atlascloud).
+    out_lines.append("provider_aliases:")
+    for name in sorted(aliases):
+        out_lines.append(f"  {json.dumps(name)}: {aliases[name]}")
+    os.makedirs("config/settings", exist_ok=True)
+    with open("config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
+        f.write("\n".join(out_lines) + "\n")
+    print("\nwrote config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml")
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

diff --git a/src/polaris_graph/roles/provider_routing.py b/src/polaris_graph/roles/provider_routing.py
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..09e4f23e

+++ b/src/polaris_graph/roles/provider_routing.py
@@ -0,0 +1,108 @@
+"""I-run11-007 (#1051): per-role OpenRouter provider routing loader.
+
+Pins every verifier role (and, via the same config, the generator) to a ranked chain of HEALTHY,
+fast providers with a deterministic fallback that NEVER routes to a broken/flaky provider — so the
+Carney demo cannot land on the slow/empty providers that caused the runs-14/15/16 Mirror blanks.
+
+The ranked order + ignore list live in `config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml`
+(generated by `scripts/diagnostics/rank_openrouter_providers.py` from live endpoint health — LAW VI:
+config, never inlined). This module only READS that config; it never makes a network call.
+
+Degrades gracefully: if the config file or the role is absent, or routing is disabled via
+`PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING=0`, returns None and the transport keeps its prior behavior
+(`require_parameters` only). The config is committed, so production gets pinned routing by default.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import os
+from pathlib import Path
+
+import yaml
+
+_DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH = "config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml"
+_ENABLE_ENV = "PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING"
+_CONFIG_PATH_ENV = "PG_PROVIDER_ROUTING_CONFIG"
+
+# Cache keyed by the RESOLVED path string so a test that repoints _CONFIG_PATH_ENV picks up its
+# fixture rather than a stale parse. A small YAML, so a per-distinct-path parse is cheap.
+_cache: dict[str, dict] = {}
+
+
+def _enabled() -> bool:
+    return os.getenv(_ENABLE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in ("1", "true", "yes", "on")
+
+
+def _full_config() -> dict:
+    path = os.getenv(_CONFIG_PATH_ENV, _DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH)
+    if path in _cache:
+        return _cache[path]
+    p = Path(path)
+    data = yaml.safe_load(p.read_text(encoding="utf-8")) if p.is_file() else {}
+    result = data if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
+    _cache[path] = result
+    return result
+
+
+def _roles_config() -> dict:
+    roles = _full_config().get("roles")
+    return roles if isinstance(roles, dict) else {}
+
+
+def slug_for_provider(provider: str | None) -> str | None:
+    """Map a served `provider` DISPLAY name (OpenRouter response field, e.g. 'AtlasCloud', 'Io Net')
+    back to the routing SLUG ('atlas-cloud', 'io-net') that `provider.order`/`ignore` use, via the
+    config's `provider_aliases` map. Falls back to a lower/space-fold for providers not in the map.
+    Returns the input unchanged if falsy. (Codex diff-gate iter-1 P1: a naive fold mis-maps camelCase
+    providers, so the empty-retry could ignore an identity OpenRouter does not match -> retry the same
+    blank provider.)"""
+    if not provider:
+        return provider
+    aliases = _full_config().get("provider_aliases")
+    if isinstance(aliases, dict) and provider in aliases:
+        return str(aliases[provider])
+    return provider.strip().lower().replace(" ", "-")
+
+
+def reset_cache() -> None:
+    """Drop the parsed-config cache (tests that swap the config fixture call this)."""
+    _cache.clear()
+
+
+def role_provider_routing(role: str) -> dict | None:
+    """Return ``{"order": [slug...], "ignore": [slug...]}`` for ``role``, else ``None``.
+
+    ``None`` means "not configured / disabled" — the caller keeps its prior provider block.
+    A configured role MUST have a non-empty ``order`` (an empty order would pin nothing); an empty
+    or missing ``ignore`` is fine.
+    """
+    if not _enabled():
+        return None
+    cfg = _roles_config().get(role)
+    if not isinstance(cfg, dict):
+        return None
+    order = [str(s) for s in (cfg.get("order") or []) if str(s).strip()]
+    if not order:
+        return None
+    ignore = [str(s) for s in (cfg.get("ignore") or []) if str(s).strip()]
+    return {"order": order, "ignore": ignore}
+
+
+def apply_provider_routing(provider_block: dict, role: str) -> dict:
+    """Merge the role's ranked order + ignore + ``allow_fallbacks: False`` into ``provider_block``.
+
+    ``allow_fallbacks: False`` (per the OpenRouter routing docs) restricts attempts to EXACTLY the
+    listed healthy providers in rank order — OpenRouter never falls through to an unlisted flaky
+    provider. ``ignore`` is the belt-and-suspenders deny-list. A pre-existing ``require_parameters``
+    is preserved. No-op (returns the block unchanged) when the role is unconfigured.
+    """
+    routing = role_provider_routing(role)
+    if routing is None:
+        return provider_block
+    provider_block["order"] = routing["order"]
+    if routing["ignore"]:
+        # merge, do not clobber, any pre-set ignore
+        existing = provider_block.get("ignore") or []
+        provider_block["ignore"] = list(dict.fromkeys([*existing, *routing["ignore"]]))
+    provider_block["allow_fallbacks"] = False
+    return provider_block

+"""I-run11-007 (#1051): OpenRouter provider-routing + empty-response failover tests.
+
+SPEND-FREE: the empty-retry test injects an `httpx.MockTransport`, so no socket / no LLM / no spend.
+Routing is exercised against a DETERMINISTIC fixture config (not the live-data file), and the
+autouse disable from `conftest.py` is overridden per-test by re-enabling + pointing at the fixture.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import json
+from pathlib import Path
+
+import httpx
+import pytest
+
+from src.polaris_graph.roles import provider_routing
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.openrouter_role_transport import OpenRouterRoleTransport
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.provider_routing import (
+    apply_provider_routing,
+    role_provider_routing,
+)
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.role_transport import RoleRequest
+
+_FIXTURE = str(Path(__file__).parent.parent / "fixtures" / "openrouter_provider_routing_fixture.yaml")
+_MIRROR_SLUG = "z-ai/glm-5.1"
+
+
+@pytest.fixture
+def _routing_on(monkeypatch):
+    """Re-enable routing (the dir conftest disables it) against the deterministic fixture config."""
+    monkeypatch.setenv("PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING", "1")
+    monkeypatch.setenv("PG_PROVIDER_ROUTING_CONFIG", _FIXTURE)
+    monkeypatch.setenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY", "test-or-key")
+    monkeypatch.delenv("PG_MIRROR_MODEL", raising=False)
+    provider_routing.reset_cache()
+    yield
+    provider_routing.reset_cache()
+
+
+def test_loader_reads_fixture(_routing_on):
+    assert role_provider_routing("mirror") == {
+        "order": ["friendli", "fireworks", "deepinfra"],
+        "ignore": ["phala", "together"],
+    }
+    assert role_provider_routing("sentinel") == {"order": ["novita", "minimax"], "ignore": []}
+
+
+def test_disabled_returns_none(monkeypatch):
+    monkeypatch.setenv("PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING", "0")
+    monkeypatch.setenv("PG_PROVIDER_ROUTING_CONFIG", _FIXTURE)
+    provider_routing.reset_cache()
+    assert role_provider_routing("mirror") is None
+
+
+def test_apply_builds_block_reasoning_role(_routing_on):
+    block = apply_provider_routing({"require_parameters": True}, "mirror")
+    assert block["order"] == ["friendli", "fireworks", "deepinfra"]
+    assert block["ignore"] == ["phala", "together"]
+    assert block["allow_fallbacks"] is False
+    # require_parameters preserved
+    assert block["require_parameters"] is True
+
+
+def test_apply_noop_when_unconfigured_role(_routing_on):
+    # a role absent from the config leaves the block untouched (no order/allow_fallbacks injected)
+    block = apply_provider_routing({"require_parameters": True}, "nonexistent_role")
+    assert block == {"require_parameters": True}
+
+
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
+# The crux of #1051: OpenRouter does NOT fall back on an empty 200, so the transport must
+# exclude the blanked provider and retry on the NEXT healthy provider itself.
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
+def _sequence_handler(responses):
+    state = {"bodies": [], "i": 0}
+
+    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
+        state["bodies"].append(json.loads(request.content.decode("utf-8")))
+        payload = responses[min(state["i"], len(responses) - 1)]
+        state["i"] += 1
+        return httpx.Response(200, json=payload)
+
+    return handler, state
+
+
+def _completion(provider: str, content: str):
+    return {
+        "model": _MIRROR_SLUG,
+        "provider": provider,
+        "choices": [{"message": {"role": "assistant", "content": content}, "finish_reason": "stop"}],
+        "usage": {"prompt_tokens": 10, "completion_tokens": 3},
+    }
+
+
+def test_empty_response_excludes_provider_and_retries(_routing_on):
+    # 1st provider returns an empty 200 (the blank); the served `provider` is the DISPLAY name
+    # "Friendli" — the retry must exclude the routing SLUG "friendli" (Codex iter-1 P1), not the
+    # display form, so OpenRouter actually advances to the next healthy provider.
+    handler, state = _sequence_handler([
+        _completion("Friendli", ""),                      # blank (DISPLAY name) -> exclude slug + retry
+        _completion("Fireworks", "<co>x</co:d1>"),        # healthy fallback
+    ])
+    transport = OpenRouterRoleTransport(httpx.Client(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler)))
+    req = RoleRequest(role="mirror", model_slug=_MIRROR_SLUG, prompt="decide", params={})
+
+    resp = transport.complete(req)
+
+    # it recovered on the 2nd provider, not a blank crash
+    assert resp.raw_text == "<co>x</co:d1>"
+    assert len(state["bodies"]) == 2
+    # 1st attempt: routed to the ranked order, friendli NOT yet ignored
+    assert "friendli" not in (state["bodies"][0]["provider"].get("ignore") or [])
+    # 2nd attempt: the blanked provider's SLUG (friendli, mapped from display "Friendli") is ignored
+    assert "friendli" in state["bodies"][1]["provider"]["ignore"]
+    # the pre-configured ignores survive the retry too
+    assert "phala" in state["bodies"][1]["provider"]["ignore"]
+
+
+def test_served_display_name_maps_to_slug(_routing_on):
+    # the camelCase / spaced display names a naive lower/space-fold would mis-map
+    from src.polaris_graph.roles.provider_routing import slug_for_provider
+
+    assert slug_for_provider("AtlasCloud") == "atlas-cloud"   # alias map (naive fold -> 'atlascloud')
+    assert slug_for_provider("Io Net") == "io-net"
+    assert slug_for_provider("Friendli") == "friendli"
+    # not in the map -> best-effort fold
+    assert slug_for_provider("SomeNewProvider") == "somenewprovider"
+    assert slug_for_provider(None) is None
```

   1: """I-run11-007 (#1051): per-role OpenRouter provider routing loader.
   2: 
   3: Pins every verifier role (and, via the same config, the generator) to a ranked chain of HEALTHY,
   4: fast providers with a deterministic fallback that NEVER routes to a broken/flaky provider — so the
   5: Carney demo cannot land on the slow/empty providers that caused the runs-14/15/16 Mirror blanks.
   6: 
   7: The ranked order + ignore list live in `config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml`
   8: (generated by `scripts/diagnostics/rank_openrouter_providers.py` from live endpoint health — LAW VI:
   9: config, never inlined). This module only READS that config; it never makes a network call.
  10: 
  11: Degrades gracefully: if the config file or the role is absent, or routing is disabled via
  12: `PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING=0`, returns None and the transport keeps its prior behavior
  13: (`require_parameters` only). The config is committed, so production gets pinned routing by default.
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: import os
  19: from pathlib import Path
  20: 
  21: import yaml
  22: 
  23: _DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH = "config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml"
  24: _ENABLE_ENV = "PG_OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ROUTING"
  25: _CONFIG_PATH_ENV = "PG_PROVIDER_ROUTING_CONFIG"
  26: 
  27: # Cache keyed by the RESOLVED path string so a test that repoints _CONFIG_PATH_ENV picks up its
  28: # fixture rather than a stale parse. A small YAML, so a per-distinct-path parse is cheap.
  29: _cache: dict[str, dict] = {}
  30: 
  31: 
  32: def _enabled() -> bool:
  33:     return os.getenv(_ENABLE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in ("1", "true", "yes", "on")
  34: 
  35: 
  36: def _full_config() -> dict:
  37:     path = os.getenv(_CONFIG_PATH_ENV, _DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH)
  38:     if path in _cache:
  39:         return _cache[path]
  40:     p = Path(path)
  41:     data = yaml.safe_load(p.read_text(encoding="utf-8")) if p.is_file() else {}
  42:     result = data if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
  43:     _cache[path] = result
  44:     return result
  45: 
  46: 
  47: def _roles_config() -> dict:
  48:     roles = _full_config().get("roles")
  49:     return roles if isinstance(roles, dict) else {}
  50: 
  51: 
  52: def slug_for_provider(provider: str | None) -> str | None:
  53:     """Map a served `provider` DISPLAY name (OpenRouter response field, e.g. 'AtlasCloud', 'Io Net')
  54:     back to the routing SLUG ('atlas-cloud', 'io-net') that `provider.order`/`ignore` use, via the
  55:     config's `provider_aliases` map. Falls back to a lower/space-fold for providers not in the map.
  56:     Returns the input unchanged if falsy. (Codex diff-gate iter-1 P1: a naive fold mis-maps camelCase
  57:     providers, so the empty-retry could ignore an identity OpenRouter does not match -> retry the same
  58:     blank provider.)"""
  59:     if not provider:
  60:         return provider
  61:     aliases = _full_config().get("provider_aliases")
  62:     if isinstance(aliases, dict) and provider in aliases:
  63:         return str(aliases[provider])
  64:     return provider.strip().lower().replace(" ", "-")
  65: 
  66: 
  67: def reset_cache() -> None:
  68:     """Drop the parsed-config cache (tests that swap the config fixture call this)."""
  69:     _cache.clear()

  71: 
  72: def role_provider_routing(role: str) -> dict | None:
  73:     """Return ``{"order": [slug...], "ignore": [slug...]}`` for ``role``, else ``None``.
  74: 
  75:     ``None`` means "not configured / disabled" — the caller keeps its prior provider block.
  76:     A configured role MUST have a non-empty ``order`` (an empty order would pin nothing); an empty
  77:     or missing ``ignore`` is fine.
  78:     """
  79:     if not _enabled():
  80:         return None
  81:     cfg = _roles_config().get(role)
  82:     if not isinstance(cfg, dict):
  83:         return None
  84:     order = [str(s) for s in (cfg.get("order") or []) if str(s).strip()]
  85:     if not order:
  86:         return None
  87:     ignore = [str(s) for s in (cfg.get("ignore") or []) if str(s).strip()]
  88:     return {"order": order, "ignore": ignore}
  89: 
  90: 
  91: def apply_provider_routing(provider_block: dict, role: str) -> dict:
  92:     """Merge the role's ranked order + ignore + ``allow_fallbacks: False`` into ``provider_block``.
  93: 
  94:     ``allow_fallbacks: False`` (per the OpenRouter routing docs) restricts attempts to EXACTLY the
  95:     listed healthy providers in rank order — OpenRouter never falls through to an unlisted flaky
  96:     provider. ``ignore`` is the belt-and-suspenders deny-list. A pre-existing ``require_parameters``
  97:     is preserved. No-op (returns the block unchanged) when the role is unconfigured.
  98:     """
  99:     routing = role_provider_routing(role)
 100:     if routing is None:
 101:         return provider_block
 102:     provider_block["order"] = routing["order"]
 103:     if routing["ignore"]:
 104:         # merge, do not clobber, any pre-set ignore
 105:         existing = provider_block.get("ignore") or []
 106:         provider_block["ignore"] = list(dict.fromkeys([*existing, *routing["ignore"]]))
 107:     provider_block["allow_fallbacks"] = False
 108:     return provider_block

 448:     """Assemble the OpenRouter request body: the SAME OpenAI-compatible body the self-host
 449:     transport builds, MINUS the top-level `documents` key (P1-4), PLUS the MAX-reasoning param.
 450: 
 451:     Reuses `_build_body` for `model` + `messages` + the explicit passthrough allowlist
 452:     (structured_outputs / response_format / documents / max_tokens — POLARIS-internal keys like
 453:     pass2_input / citations / system never reach the body). Then (P1-4) DROPS the top-level
 454:     `documents` key, which OpenRouter's chat-completions schema does not define and which would
 455:     fail routing under `provider.require_parameters=True` — the evidence is already rendered into
 456:     `messages` by `_normalize_messages`, so model-visibility is preserved. Then sets
 457:     `reasoning = {"enabled": True, "effort": <_REASONING_EFFORT>}` — the openrouter_client
 458:     `reasoning_enabled` shape (openrouter_client.py:1424). Per OpenRouter docs the mutually
 459:     exclusive pair is `reasoning.effort` vs `reasoning.max_tokens`; the TOP-LEVEL `max_tokens` is
 460:     NOT exclusive with effort and MUST exceed the reasoning budget. Under `effort=xhigh` the
 461:     provider spends ~95% of top-level `max_tokens` on reasoning, so a popped/absent `max_tokens`
 462:     starves the verdict. I-meta-008 FULL-POWER therefore SETS a generous top-level `max_tokens`
 463:     (PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS, default 16384) for the reasoning verifiers and an explicit
 464:     small classifier budget (PG_SENTINEL_MAX_TOKENS, default 256) for the non-reasoning Sentinel.
 465:     Source: https://openrouter.ai/docs/guides/best-practices/reasoning-tokens
 466:     """
 467:     body = _build_body(request, model_slug, normalized_messages)
 468:     # P1-4: strip OpenRouter-unsupported top-level keys (currently `documents`). The evidence is
 469:     # already model-visible in `messages` (rendered by `_normalize_messages`), so the model still
 470:     # sees it; this only removes the schema-invalid body key that breaks require_parameters routing.
 471:     for key in _OPENROUTER_UNSUPPORTED_TOP_LEVEL_KEYS:
 472:         body.pop(key, None)
 473:     # Codex iter-2 P1: reasoning is PER-ROLE. Only the deliberative verifiers (Mirror/Judge) get
 474:     # MAX reasoning + `provider.require_parameters=True`. The Sentinel classifier gets NEITHER —
 475:     # its OpenRouter slug does not advertise `reasoning`, so `require_parameters=True` would refuse
 476:     # to route and fail the first call. See `role_reasoning_enabled` for the full rationale.
 477:     if role_reasoning_enabled(request.role, request.model_slug):
 478:         body["reasoning"] = {"enabled": True, "effort": _REASONING_EFFORT}
 479:         # require_parameters=True makes OpenRouter ONLY route to a provider that actually HONORS the
 480:         # `reasoning` param (OpenRouter's default when absent is False — it could otherwise route a
 481:         # verifier to a provider that silently IGNORES reasoning, defeating the operator's
 482:         # MAX-reasoning purpose). Mirrors openrouter_client._call_impl's provider block
 483:         # (openrouter_client.py:1484-1487, OPENROUTER_REQUIRE_PARAMETERS default "true"). The
 484:         # I-bug-946 singleton-routing half (resolved per-role provider) is M4/PENDING and
 485:         # intentionally NOT here.
 486:         # I-run11-007 (#1051): pin to the ranked HEALTHY provider chain (order + ignore +
 487:         # allow_fallbacks:False) so a verifier call never lands on a slow/flaky provider.
 488:         body["provider"] = apply_provider_routing({"require_parameters": True}, request.role)
 489:         # I-meta-008 FULL-POWER (CORRECTS #1017): a reasoning verifier MUST carry a GENEROUS top-level
 490:         # `max_tokens`, NOT have it popped. OpenRouter `effort=xhigh` allocates ~95% of `max_tokens`
 491:         # to the reasoning budget, and `max_tokens` MUST be strictly higher than that budget so the
 492:         # bare verdict has room (docs: best-practices/reasoning-tokens). It is `reasoning.effort` vs
 493:         # `reasoning.max_tokens` that are mutually exclusive — NOT top-level `max_tokens`. The prior
 494:         # #1017 fix popped it, so xhigh ate ~95% of an unknown provider default and STARVED the verdict
 495:         # to empty for a reasoning-first Mirror (GLM-5.1) / Judge (Qwen) -> fail-loud crash on the run.
 496:         # 16384 -> reasoning ~15564 + verdict room ~820 (generous for Mirror JSON + Judge enum).
 497:         #
 498:         # I-run11-004: the DECOMPOSITION Sentinel (MiniMax-M2, reasoning ON) emits a JSON
 499:         # {verdict, unsupported_atoms, atoms} body — a multi-atom list needs MORE output room than a
 500:         # bare verdict, AND the certification used reasoning + max_tokens>=3000. So the decomposition
 501:         # Sentinel gets its OWN generous budget (default 16384, hard-floored at 3000 so an env
 502:         # override can never re-introduce the run-12 truncation that collapses every claim to a
 503:         # fail-closed UNGROUNDED). Other reasoning verifiers keep PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS.
 504:         if request.role == "sentinel":
 505:             decomp_budget = int(os.getenv("PG_SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MAX_TOKENS", "16384"))
 506:             body["max_tokens"] = max(decomp_budget, _SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MIN_MAX_TOKENS)
 507:         else:
 508:             body["max_tokens"] = int(os.getenv("PG_VERIFIER_REASONING_MAX_TOKENS", "16384"))
 509:     else:
 510:         # Sentinel (reasoning-disabled classifier): give it explicit output room rather than relying
 511:         # on an unknown provider default (no pop-and-hope). Small budget is plenty for a label verdict.
 512:         body["max_tokens"] = int(os.getenv("PG_SENTINEL_MAX_TOKENS", "256"))
 513:         # I-run11-007 (#1051): pin the non-reasoning role to its ranked HEALTHY provider chain too
 514:         # (NO require_parameters — its slug does not advertise reasoning, so require_parameters would
 515:         # refuse to route). Only set the block when routing is configured for the role.
 516:         routed = apply_provider_routing({}, request.role)
 517:         if routed:
 518:             body["provider"] = routed
 519:     return body

 522: def _openrouter_served_block(raw: dict) -> dict:
 523:     """Stash the genuinely-OpenRouter-served identity under `_pathb_served` for the M4
 524:     served==pinned gate.
 525: 
 526:     OpenRouter reports the served `provider` / `model` / `system_fingerprint` at the top level
 527:     of the response body (unlike a self-host vLLM, whose served identity is its `endpoint`). We
 528:     surface exactly those three, dropping any that are absent — `build_response_metadata`
 529:     consumes `provider`/`model`/`system_fingerprint` from `_pathb_served` and never substitutes
 530:     a request-derived value, so a response that fails to report its served identity fails the
 531:     gate loud rather than passing on request-derived data.
 532:     """
 533:     served: dict = {}
 534:     for key in ("provider", "model", "system_fingerprint"):
 535:         value = raw.get(key)
 536:         if value:
 537:             served[key] = value
 538:     return served

 541: def _parse_openrouter_response(raw: dict) -> tuple[object, str | None, dict | None, str | None]:
 542:     """OpenRouter-aware `(raw_text, served_model, usage, reasoning)` extraction (P1-3).
 543: 
 544:     Identical fail-loud contract to the self-host `_parse_response` (a missing `choices`, a
 545:     non-dict choice / message, or a blank bare verdict after reasoning separation raises
 546:     `RoleTransportError` — an empty/blank/reasoning-only completion is never a valid verifier
 547:     answer). The ONLY difference is the reasoning-extraction precedence: OpenRouter returns the
 548:     verifier's chain-of-thought in `message.reasoning` (NOT `reasoning_content`, NOT an inline
 549:     `<think>` block) per https://openrouter.ai/docs/guides/best-practices/reasoning-tokens . So
 550:     the precedence here is: `reasoning_content` (vLLM reasoning-parser shape, kept for
 551:     cross-provider safety) -> `message.reasoning` (OpenRouter shape) -> a leading inline
 552:     `<think>` block split off `content`.
 553: 
 554:     Reasoning stays SEPARATE from `raw_text` (I-meta-002-q1b): `raw_text` is ONLY the bare
 555:     verdict/body the verdict parsers consume; the reasoning rides on `RoleResponse.reasoning`.
 556:     """
 557:     choices = raw.get("choices")
 558:     if not choices:
 559:         raise RoleTransportError(
 560:             f"OpenRouter response carried no choices (model={raw.get('model')!r})"
 561:         )
 562:     first_choice = choices[0]
 563:     if not isinstance(first_choice, dict):
 564:         raise RoleTransportError(
 565:             f"OpenRouter response choice was not an object (model={raw.get('model')!r})"
 566:         )
 567:     message = first_choice.get("message")
 568:     if not isinstance(message, dict):
 569:         raise RoleTransportError(
 570:             f"OpenRouter response choice carried no message object (model={raw.get('model')!r})"
 571:         )
 572:     content = message.get("content")
 573:     model_repr = f"{raw.get('model')!r}"
 574: 
 575:     # Reasoning precedence: explicit separate fields first (content is already the bare verdict),
 576:     # then a leading inline <think> block. `reasoning_content` is the vLLM reasoning-parser field;
 577:     # `reasoning` is OpenRouter's documented field (P1-3). Either separate field means `content`
 578:     # is the bare verdict and is NOT searched for a <think> block.
 579:     reasoning_content = message.get("reasoning_content")
 580:     openrouter_reasoning = message.get("reasoning")
 581:     if isinstance(reasoning_content, str) and reasoning_content.strip():
 582:         bare: object = content
 583:         reasoning: str | None = reasoning_content
 584:     elif isinstance(openrouter_reasoning, str) and openrouter_reasoning.strip():
 585:         bare = content
 586:         reasoning = openrouter_reasoning
 587:     else:
 588:         bare, reasoning = _separate_reasoning(content, model_repr)
 589: 
 590:     # Post-split blank guard (same as _parse_response): a verifier role MUST return a non-blank
 591:     # bare verdict/body. A reasoning-only / think-only / empty-content response is a transport
 592:     # failure, never a deliberately-empty answer — fail loud.
 593:     if bare is None or (isinstance(bare, str) and not bare.strip()):
 594:         # I-meta-008 / #1026: a RECOVERABLE blank — a reasoning-first verifier under effort=xhigh
 595:         # can exhaust its reasoning budget without converging and emit zero content. Raise the
 596:         # distinct BlankVerdictError so `complete()` retries with the reasoning effort stepped DOWN
 597:         # (forcing the bare verdict) instead of hard-crashing the whole 4-role run. Still fail-loud
 598:         # if every step-down also blanks.
 599:         raise BlankVerdictError(
 600:             f"OpenRouter response choice carried no/blank message content after reasoning "
 601:             f"separation (model={model_repr})"
 602:         )
 603:     served_model = raw.get("model")
 604:     usage = raw.get("usage")
 605:     return bare, served_model, usage, reasoning

 608: class OpenRouterRoleTransport:
 609:     """Sync `RoleTransport` routing the Mirror / Sentinel / Judge verifier roles via OpenRouter
 610:     with MAX reasoning (benchmark stage, I-meta-007d).
 611: 
 612:     Implements the SAME `RoleTransport` Protocol as `OpenAICompatibleRoleTransport`. The
 613:     `httpx.Client` is INJECTED so tests pass an in-process stub (no network, no spend). Each
 614:     `complete()` resolves the OpenRouter endpoint + BENCHMARK-lineup slug (P1-1), normalizes the
 615:     payload (reusing the self-host message-rendering, then dropping the top-level `documents` key
 616:     per P1-4), POSTs `/chat/completions` with MAX (`xhigh`) reasoning enabled, separates reasoning
 617:     from the bare verdict (via `_parse_openrouter_response`, which reads `message.reasoning` per
 618:     P1-3), captures the call under the Path-B gate (reasoning sanitized OUT of the capture
 619:     channel), and returns a `RoleResponse` with reasoning kept SEPARATE from `raw_text`.
 620: 
 621:     SOVEREIGNTY: OpenRouter is a US router — dev/benchmark ONLY. Self-host (the lock's
 622:     `serving_route`) is the final sovereign destination. See the module docstring.
 623:     """
 624: 
 625:     def __init__(self, http_client: httpx.Client) -> None:
 626:         self._http_client = http_client
 627: 
 628:     def complete(self, request: RoleRequest) -> RoleResponse:
 629:         """Perform one OpenRouter completion for `request`. SYNC. Fails loud on error.
 630: 
 631:         Generator requests raise via `openrouter_role_endpoint`. The normalized messages are the
 632:         SAME list POSTed to the body AND passed to `capture_llm_call`. The captured raw is
 633:         augmented with `_pathb_served={provider, model, system_fingerprint}` so M4's
 634:         served==pinned check consumes the genuinely-served OpenRouter identity (not the
 635:         request-derived `model`). Reasoning is separated from the bare verdict (I-meta-002-q1b)
 636:         and sanitized OUT of the Path-B capture channel.
 637:         """
 638:         base_url, api_key, model_slug = openrouter_role_endpoint(request.role)
 639:         normalized_messages = _normalize_messages(request)
 640:         body = _build_openrouter_body(request, model_slug, normalized_messages)
 641:         url = f"{base_url}{_CHAT_COMPLETIONS_PATH}"
 642:         headers = {
 643:             "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
 644:             "Content-Type": "application/json",
 645:             "HTTP-Referer": "https://polaris-research.ai",
 646:             "X-Title": "polaris graph",
 647:         }
 648: 
 649:         # I-meta-008 / #1026: reasoning verifiers get the blank-verdict step-down ladder so a
 650:         # non-converging xhigh response cannot crash the whole 4-role run. The non-reasoning
 651:         # Sentinel makes a SINGLE attempt (its body has no `reasoning` block to step down) — its
 652:         # behavior is unchanged.
 653:         reasoning_role = role_reasoning_enabled(request.role, request.model_slug)
 654:         # I-run11-007 (#1051): a NON-reasoning role made a SINGLE attempt, so a blank from a flaky
 655:         # provider had no recovery (OpenRouter does not auto-advance on an empty 200). When the role
 656:         # is PINNED to a ranked provider chain, give it (1 + PG_PROVIDER_BLANK_RETRIES) attempts at
 657:         # the same effort; each blank excludes the served provider so the retry advances to the next
 658:         # HEALTHY provider. WITHOUT routing there is no chain to fail over to, so it keeps the original
 659:         # single attempt (the reasoning-roles-only step-down ladder is unchanged when routing is off).
 660:         provider_blank_retries = max(0, int(os.getenv("PG_PROVIDER_BLANK_RETRIES", "3")))
 661:         role_is_routed = role_provider_routing(request.role) is not None
 662:         non_reasoning_attempts = (1 + provider_blank_retries) if role_is_routed else 1
 663:         effort_ladder: tuple[object, ...] = (
 664:             _VERIFIER_EFFORT_LADDER
 665:             if reasoning_role
 666:             else (_REASONING_EFFORT,) * non_reasoning_attempts
 667:         )
 668:         last_blank: BlankVerdictError | None = None
 669: 
 670:         with _pathb_capture.llm_role(request.role):
 671:             for attempt, effort in enumerate(effort_ladder):
 672:                 # Step the reasoning effort DOWN per attempt (only meaningful for a reasoning role,
 673:                 # whose body carries a `reasoning` block). `effort is None` => reasoning DISABLED
 674:                 # (final resort, guarantees content): drop the `reasoning` param. Keep
 675:                 # `provider.require_parameters` if the body STILL carries an output-constraining
 676:                 # param (`response_format` / `structured_outputs`) — that pin then guarantees a
 677:                 # provider that HONORS those constraints (Codex diff-gate P2). Only when reasoning
 678:                 # was the sole constrained param do we drop require_parameters (it would otherwise
 679:                 # have nothing to enforce).
 680:                 if reasoning_role and "reasoning" in body:
 681:                     if effort is None:
 682:                         body.pop("reasoning", None)
 683:                         provider = body.get("provider")
 684:                         if isinstance(provider, dict) and not (
 685:                             "response_format" in body or "structured_outputs" in body
 686:                         ):
 687:                             provider.pop("require_parameters", None)
 688:                             if not provider:
 689:                                 body.pop("provider", None)
 690:                     else:
 691:                         body["reasoning"] = {"enabled": True, "effort": effort}
 692: 
 693:                 try:
 694:                     http_response = self._http_client.post(
 695:                         url, json=body, headers=headers, timeout=_TIMEOUT_SECONDS
 696:                     )
 697:                 except httpx.HTTPError as exc:
 698:                     raise RoleTransportError(
 699:                         f"OpenRouter {request.role!r} transport error at {url}: {exc}"
 700:                     ) from exc
 701: 
 702:                 if http_response.status_code != httpx.codes.OK:
 703:                     raise RoleTransportError(
 704:                         f"OpenRouter {request.role!r} returned HTTP {http_response.status_code} "
 705:                         f"at {url}"
 706:                     )
 707:                 try:
 708:                     raw = http_response.json()
 709:                 except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError) as exc:
 710:                     raise RoleTransportError(
 711:                         f"OpenRouter {request.role!r} returned a non-JSON body at {url}: {exc}"
 712:                     ) from exc
 713: 
 714:                 # I-meta-002-q1b + P1-3: reasoning separated from the bare verdict HERE via the
 715:                 # OpenRouter-aware parser (reads `message.reasoning`, not just `reasoning_content` /
 716:                 # `<think>`), so the verdict parsers only ever see the bare answer (no "soap") and
 717:                 # the OpenRouter reasoning is not lost. A BLANK bare verdict is RECOVERABLE (#1026):
 718:                 # step the effort down and retry; fail loud only if the ladder is exhausted.
 719:                 try:
 720:                     raw_text, served_model, usage, reasoning = _parse_openrouter_response(raw)
 721:                 except BlankVerdictError as exc:
 722:                     last_blank = exc
 723:                     # Codex diff-gate P1 (budget-cap bypass): a blank attempt is DISCARDED, so its
 724:                     # `usage` never reaches RecordingTransport (which bills only the final returned
 725:                     # response). Account THIS blank attempt's tokens into the SAME shared
 726:                     # PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN accumulator the generator + the successful verifier calls
 727:                     # feed, then enforce the cap BEFORE the next paid retry. Lazy import keeps the
 728:                     # raw transport free of an import-time dependency on the orchestration layer
 729:                     # (`compute_role_call_cost` lives in role_pipeline; `_orc` is openrouter_client,
 730:                     # which does NOT import the roles package — both are cycle-safe).
 731:                     import src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client as _orc
 732:                     from src.polaris_graph.roles.role_pipeline import compute_role_call_cost
 733: 
 734:                     _orc._add_run_cost(
 735:                         compute_role_call_cost(request.model_slug, raw.get("usage"))
 736:                     )
 737:                     _orc.check_run_budget(0)  # raises BudgetExceededError if the cap is now crossed.
 738:                     # I-run11-007 (#1051): exclude the provider that just returned blank so the NEXT
 739:                     # attempt advances to the next HEALTHY provider in the ranked order (OpenRouter
 740:                     # will NOT auto-advance on an empty 200). The served `provider` is the DISPLAY
 741:                     # name; map it back to the routing SLUG so `ignore` uses the SAME identity as
 742:                     # `order` (Codex diff-gate iter-1 P1). Persists across the reasoning step-down too.
 743:                     blanked_provider = slug_for_provider(raw.get("provider"))
 744:                     if blanked_provider and isinstance(body.get("provider"), dict):
 745:                         ignore_list = body["provider"].setdefault("ignore", [])
 746:                         if blanked_provider not in ignore_list:
 747:                             ignore_list.append(blanked_provider)
 748:                     if attempt + 1 < len(effort_ladder):
 749:                         logger.warning(
 750:                             "[polaris graph] #1026: %s blank verdict at reasoning effort=%s "
 751:                             "(attempt %d/%d) — stepping effort down to %s and retrying.",
 752:                             request.role, effort, attempt + 1, len(effort_ladder),
 753:                             effort_ladder[attempt + 1],
 754:                         )
 755:                         continue
 756:                     raise  # ladder exhausted: even reasoning-off blanked -> genuine fail-loud.
 757: 
 758:                 # Stash the genuinely-OpenRouter-served identity for M4 BEFORE capture, then
 759:                 # sanitize reasoning OUT of the captured response (no-leak): reasoning lives ONLY
 760:                 # on the returned RoleResponse + four_role_role_calls.jsonl, never in the capture
 761:                 # channel.
 762:                 raw["_pathb_served"] = _openrouter_served_block(raw)
 763:                 _pathb_capture.capture_llm_call(
 764:                     role=request.role,
 765:                     messages=normalized_messages,
 766:                     raw_response=_sanitize_raw_for_capture(raw, bare_text=raw_text),
 767:                 )

  70: # --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  71: # The crux of #1051: OpenRouter does NOT fall back on an empty 200, so the transport must
  72: # exclude the blanked provider and retry on the NEXT healthy provider itself.
  73: # --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  74: def _sequence_handler(responses):
  75:     state = {"bodies": [], "i": 0}
  76: 
  77:     def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
  78:         state["bodies"].append(json.loads(request.content.decode("utf-8")))
  79:         payload = responses[min(state["i"], len(responses) - 1)]
  80:         state["i"] += 1
  81:         return httpx.Response(200, json=payload)
  82: 
  83:     return handler, state
  84: 
  85: 
  86: def _completion(provider: str, content: str):
  87:     return {
  88:         "model": _MIRROR_SLUG,
  89:         "provider": provider,
  90:         "choices": [{"message": {"role": "assistant", "content": content}, "finish_reason": "stop"}],
  91:         "usage": {"prompt_tokens": 10, "completion_tokens": 3},
  92:     }
  93:

   1: #!/usr/bin/env python3
   2: """I-run11-007 (#1051): rank each role model's OpenRouter providers by STABILITY + SPEED and emit
   3: config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml — the ranked, healthy-only provider order used to
   4: pin every LLM to a stable+fast provider with a deterministic fallback chain that NEVER routes to a
   5: broken server.
   6: 
   7: Ranking (per the research on /docs provider-selection): keep only operational endpoints
   8: (status==0), then sort by uptime_last_30m desc, latency_last_30m asc, throughput_last_30m desc.
   9: The `order` list is the ranked healthy chain (used with allow_fallbacks:false so off-list flaky
  10: providers are never tried). The `ignore` list is the explicit deny-list of broken endpoints
  11: (status!=0 or uptime below the floor) as belt-and-suspenders.
  12: 
  13: Reads OPENROUTER_API_KEY from env/.env (never printed). Deterministic given live data. Run from repo root.
  14: """
  15: from __future__ import annotations
  16: import json, os, sys, urllib.request
  17: 
  18: UPTIME_FLOOR = float(os.getenv("PG_PROVIDER_UPTIME_FLOOR", "98.0"))
  19: TOP_N = int(os.getenv("PG_PROVIDER_ORDER_TOP_N", "6"))
  20: ROLE_MODELS = {
  21:     "generator": "deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro",
  22:     "mirror": "z-ai/glm-5.1",
  23:     "sentinel": "minimax/minimax-m2",
  24:     "judge": "qwen/qwen3.6-35b-a3b",
  25: }
  26: 
  27: key = os.getenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
  28: if not key:
  29:     for line in open(".env", encoding="utf-8"):
  30:         if line.startswith("OPENROUTER_API_KEY="):
  31:             key = line.split("=", 1)[1].strip().strip('"').strip("'"); break
  32: if not key:
  33:     print("NO OPENROUTER_API_KEY"); sys.exit(2)
  34: 
  35: 
  36: def endpoints(model: str) -> list[dict]:
  37:     req = urllib.request.Request(
  38:         f"https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models/{model}/endpoints",
  39:         headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"},
  40:     )
  41:     return json.loads(urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=30).read())["data"].get("endpoints", [])
  42: 
  43: 
  44: def rank(eps: list[dict]) -> tuple[list[str], list[str], list[str]]:
  45:     healthy, broken = [], []
  46:     for e in eps:
  47:         up = e.get("uptime_last_30m")
  48:         operational = e.get("status") == 0 and (up is None or up >= UPTIME_FLOOR)
  49:         (healthy if operational else broken).append(e)
  50: 
  51:     def p50(v):
  52:         # latency/throughput are percentile dicts {p50,p75,p90,p99}; a scalar or None is tolerated.
  53:         if isinstance(v, dict):
  54:             return v.get("p50")
  55:         return v
  56: 
  57:     def sort_key(e: dict):
  58:         # Stability is already GATED (uptime>=floor + status==0). Among the stable set, rank by SPEED:
  59:         # throughput p50 desc PRIMARY (our verifier calls are reasoning-heavy = long outputs, so
  60:         # tokens/sec dominates total time), latency p50 asc secondary (time-to-first-token), uptime
  61:         # desc final tiebreak. None metrics rank last. -> "stable (gated) AND fastest (sorted)".
  62:         tput = p50(e.get("throughput_last_30m"))
  63:         lat = p50(e.get("latency_last_30m"))
  64:         up = e.get("uptime_last_30m")
  65:         return (
  66:             -(tput if tput is not None else -1.0),
  67:             (lat if lat is not None else float("inf")),
  68:             -(up if up is not None else -1.0),
  69:         )
  70: 
  71:     def slug(e: dict) -> str:
  72:         # OpenRouter provider.order/ignore expects the provider SLUG (the `tag` prefix before '/',
  73:         # e.g. 'deepinfra/fp4' -> 'deepinfra'), NOT the display provider_name ('DeepInfra' / 'Io Net').
  74:         tag = e.get("tag") or ""
  75:         return tag.split("/")[0] if tag else (e.get("provider_name") or "").lower().replace(" ", "-")
  76: 
  77:     healthy.sort(key=sort_key)
  78: 
  79:     def dedup(eps_list: list[dict]) -> list[str]:
  80:         # a provider may expose several quant endpoints; keep its FIRST (best-ranked) slug only.
  81:         seen, out = set(), []
  82:         for e in eps_list:
  83:             s = slug(e)
  84:             if s and s not in seen:
  85:                 seen.add(s); out.append(s)
  86:         return out
  87: 
  88:     order = dedup(healthy)[:TOP_N]
  89:     ignore = [s for s in dedup(broken) if s not in set(order)]
  90:     notes = []
  91:     if len(healthy) < 3:
  92:         notes.append(f"THIN POOL: only {len(healthy)} healthy provider(s)")
  93:     if any(e.get("uptime_last_30m") is None for e in healthy):
  94:         notes.append("some providers have NULL uptime (ranked last)")
  95:     return order, ignore, notes
  96: 
  97: 
  98: def _slug_of(e: dict) -> str:
  99:     tag = e.get("tag") or ""
 100:     return tag.split("/")[0] if tag else (e.get("provider_name") or "").lower().replace(" ", "-")
 101: 
 102:

 104:     out_lines = [
 105:         "# I-run11-007 (#1051): per-role OpenRouter provider routing — ranked HEALTHY chain.",
 106:         "# Generated by scripts/diagnostics/rank_openrouter_providers.py from live endpoint health.",
 107:         f"# Ranking: status==0 + uptime_last_30m>={UPTIME_FLOOR}, sorted uptime desc / latency asc / throughput desc.",
 108:         "# Used with allow_fallbacks:false so off-list (flaky) providers are NEVER tried.",
 109:         "# Re-generate before a demo to refresh health. LAW VI: consumed as config, never inlined.",
 110:         "roles:",
 111:     ]
 112:     print(f"floor={UPTIME_FLOOR} top_n={TOP_N}\n")
 113:     aliases: dict[str, str] = {}  # served display provider_name -> routing slug (for empty-retry exclusion)
 114:     for role, model in ROLE_MODELS.items():
 115:         try:
 116:             eps = endpoints(model)
 117:         except Exception as ex:  # noqa: BLE001
 118:             print(f"{role} {model}: FETCH ERROR {str(ex)[:80]}"); continue
 119:         for e in eps:
 120:             name = e.get("provider_name")
 121:             if name:
 122:                 aliases.setdefault(name, _slug_of(e))
 123:         order, ignore, notes = rank(eps)
 124:         print(f"{role:10} ({model}): order={order}  ignore={ignore}  {notes}")
 125:         out_lines += [
 126:             f"  {role}:",
 127:             f"    model: {model}",
 128:             f"    order: [{', '.join(order)}]",
 129:             f"    ignore: [{', '.join(ignore)}]",
 130:         ]
 131:         if notes:
 132:             out_lines.append(f"    notes: \"{'; '.join(notes)}\"")
 133:     # provider_aliases: maps the served display `provider` (e.g. 'AtlasCloud', 'Io Net') back to the
 134:     # routing slug ('atlas-cloud', 'io-net') so the empty-retry excludes the SAME identity that
 135:     # `provider.ignore`/`order` use (Codex diff-gate iter-1 P1 — a naive lower/space-fold mis-maps
 136:     # camelCase providers like AtlasCloud -> atlascloud).
 137:     out_lines.append("provider_aliases:")
 138:     for name in sorted(aliases):
 139:         out_lines.append(f"  {json.dumps(name)}: {aliases[name]}")
 140:     os.makedirs("config/settings", exist_ok=True)
 141:     with open("config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
 142:         f.write("\n".join(out_lines) + "\n")
 143:     print("\nwrote config/settings/openrouter_provider_routing.yaml")

 succeeded in 992ms:
 281: # {verdict, atoms} mid-emission (the run-12 truncator) and collapses every claim to a fail-closed
 282: # UNGROUNDED. An env override (PG_SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MAX_TOKENS) can RAISE but never lower past
 283: # this floor.
 284: _SENTINEL_DECOMPOSITION_MIN_MAX_TOKENS = 3000
 285: 
 286: # I-meta-008 / #1026: blank-verdict step-down ladder. When a reasoning-first verifier returns a
 287: # BLANK bare verdict (reasoning budget exhausted without converging under the high effort), retry
 288: # with the effort stepped DOWN this ladder so the model is forced to spend tokens on the VERDICT,
 289: # not endless reasoning. The first entry is the configured MAX effort; `None` means reasoning
 290: # DISABLED (final resort — guarantees content). Overridable via PG_FOUR_ROLE_EFFORT_LADDER
 291: # (comma-separated; the literal "off"/"none" -> reasoning disabled). MAX-reasoning-first, then a
 292: # guaranteed verdict, then fail-loud only if even reasoning-off blanks.
 293: def _parse_effort_ladder() -> tuple[object, ...]:
 294:     raw = os.getenv("PG_FOUR_ROLE_EFFORT_LADDER")
 295:     if not raw:
 296:         return (_REASONING_EFFORT, "low", None)
 297:     out: list[object] = []
 298:     for token in raw.split(","):
 299:         t = token.strip()
 300:         if not t:
 301:             continue
 302:         out.append(None if t.lower() in ("off", "none", "disabled") else t)
 303:     return tuple(out) if out else (_REASONING_EFFORT, "low", None)
 304: 
 305: 
 306: _VERIFIER_EFFORT_LADDER = _parse_effort_ladder()
 307: 
 308: # Per-role reasoning policy (Codex iter-2 P1 — reasoning is NOT a one-size-fits-all switch).
 309: #
 310: # WHY per-role: Mirror (`z-ai/glm-5.1`) and Judge (`qwen/qwen3.6-35b-a3b`) are DELIBERATIVE
 311: # verifiers — they weigh evidence and argue a verdict, so they get MAX reasoning effort
 312: # (`xhigh`) AND `provider.require_parameters=True` (only route to a provider that honors
 313: # reasoning).
 314: #
 315: # Sentinel is MODE-AWARE (I-run11-004): the CERTIFIED MiniMax-M2 DECOMPOSITION Sentinel
 316: # (`minimax/minimax-m2`, the benchmark + lock default) was certified WITH reasoning ON and
 317: # max_tokens>=3000 — turning reasoning OFF (or starving max_tokens to the 256 classifier budget)
 318: # truncates the JSON {verdict, atoms} mid-emission and collapses every claim to a fail-closed
 319: # UNGROUNDED (the run-12 truncator). So when the active Sentinel groundedness mode is
 320: # "decomposition", the Sentinel sends MAX reasoning + a GENEROUS max_tokens, exactly replicating
 321: # the certified call. The SOVEREIGN `guardian`/`noninverted` granite Sentinel modes stay
 322: # reasoning-OFF (a <score>/one-word classifier whose self-host slug does not advertise
 323: # `reasoning`); their settings are NOT regressed. LAW VI: overridable via `PG_SENTINEL_REASONING`.
 324: _ROLE_REASONING_DEFAULT = {"mirror": True, "sentinel": False, "judge": True}
 325: 
 326:

 352:     """Whether the given verifier role should send the MAX-reasoning request params.
 353: 
 354:     Returns the per-role default from `_ROLE_REASONING_DEFAULT`, overridable per role via the
 355:     env var `PG_<ROLE>_REASONING` (LAW VI): "1"/"true"/"yes" -> True, "0"/"false"/"no" -> False;
 356:     absent (or any other value) falls back to the role default. Mirror/Judge default True
 357:     (deliberative verifiers -> MAX reasoning). Sentinel is MODE-AWARE (I-run11-004): in
 358:     "decomposition" mode (the certified MiniMax-M2 detector) it defaults True (reasoning ON, as
 359:     certified); in the sovereign granite `guardian`/`noninverted` modes it defaults False (a
 360:     classifier whose slug does not advertise `reasoning`, so reasoning would break routing).
 361:     """

 366:     else:

 370:         return default

 374:     if token in ("0", "false", "no"):

 180: 
 181: def _family_from_slug(slug: str) -> str:
 182:     """The family lineage of an OpenRouter slug = its `provider/` prefix (fail loud if absent).
 183: 
 184:     Every OpenRouter slug is `provider/model`; the provider prefix IS the family lineage the
 185:     4-distinct-family invariant is asserted over (z-ai / ibm-granite / qwen / deepseek). A slug
 186:     with no `/` cannot have its family determined — raise rather than guess (LAW II fail-loud).
 187:     """
 188:     provider, sep, _ = slug.partition("/")
 189:     if not sep or not provider:
 190:         raise ValueError(
 191:             f"benchmark verifier slug {slug!r} is not a `provider/model` OpenRouter slug; its "
 192:             "family lineage cannot be determined (fail-closed — the 4-distinct-family invariant "
 193:             "must assert on a real family)."
 194:         )
 195:     return provider
 196: 
 197: 
 198: def benchmark_verifier_slug(role: str) -> str:
 199:     """Resolve a verifier role's BENCHMARK-STAGE OpenRouter slug (P1-1, LAW VI).
 200: 
 201:     Sources `PG_<ROLE>_MODEL` (the lock's per-role `env_vars.primary`), DEFAULTING to the
 202:     operator-chosen role_selection_final.md OpenRouter slug. This is the benchmark lineup —
 203:     DISTINCT from the lock's self-host `_lock_model_slug` for Mirror + Sentinel (see module
 204:     docstring). The generator/unknown role raises (it is not served by this transport).
 205:     """
 206:     if role == _EXCLUDED_ROLE:
 207:         raise ValueError(
 208:             f"role {role!r} is not served by this transport — the generator runs on OpenRouter "
 209:             "via openrouter_client.py, upstream of the per-claim verifier path."
 210:         )
 211:     if role not in _SERVED_ROLES:
 212:         raise ValueError(
 213:             f"role {role!r} is not a benchmark-stage verifier role {_SERVED_ROLES}"
 214:         )
 215:     return os.getenv(_BENCHMARK_LINEUP_ENV[role], _BENCHMARK_LINEUP_DEFAULT_SLUG[role])
 216: 
 217: 
 218: def benchmark_verifier_lineup() -> dict[str, str]:
 219:     """Return the active `{mirror,sentinel,judge: benchmark_slug}` map (P1-1, LAW VI).
 220: 
 221:     The SINGLE source of truth for the benchmark-stage verifier slugs, consumed by BOTH the
 222:     transport's `openrouter_role_endpoint` (the slug it POSTs as `body["model"]`) AND
 223:     run_gate_b.py's `verifier_model_slugs` (the slug it pins into `RoleRequest.model_slug`), so
 224:     served (the slug sent) == pinned (the slug in the request/gate) on the OpenRouter path.
 225:     """
 226:     return {role: benchmark_verifier_slug(role) for role in _SERVED_ROLES}
 227: 
 228: 
 229: def benchmark_verifier_family(role: str) -> str:
 230:     """Return the ACTIVE BENCHMARK-lineup family for a verifier `role` (the active-lineup family
 231:     the 4-distinct-family check asserts on, NOT the lock's). The generator/unknown role raises.
 232: 
 233:     The family is derived from the ACTIVE slug (`benchmark_verifier_slug`, which honors the
 234:     `PG_<ROLE>_MODEL` override) — NOT a static assumption. FAILS LOUD when an override's family
 235:     leaves the role's expected default lane, so a cross-family re-pick (e.g.
 236:     `PG_JUDGE_MODEL=z-ai/glm-5.1`, which would collide the Judge with the z-ai Mirror) is caught
 237:     here rather than silently passing the 4-distinct-family gate on a stale static map
 238:     (clinical-lethal self-verify, CLAUDE.md §9.1). An IN-LANE override (same provider prefix)
 239:     passes.
 240:     """
 241:     if role == _EXCLUDED_ROLE:
 242:         raise ValueError(
 243:             f"role {role!r} is the generator — its family is sourced from the lock, not the "
 244:             "benchmark verifier lineup."
 245:         )

  79: _FLOOR_PROMPT_TOKENS = 500

  83: def compute_role_call_cost(model_slug: str, usage: dict[str, Any] | None) -> float:
  84:     """Cost (USD) for ONE verifier completion from its OpenRouter `usage` block.
  85: 
  86:     Mirrors the GENERATOR extraction (`openrouter_client._finalize_*`, :1717-1751) exactly,
  87:     because `RoleResponse.usage` is the verbatim OpenRouter usage block (same shape):
  88: 
  89:     * prompt/completion tokens read directly; **reasoning tokens are NESTED** under
  90:       `completion_tokens_details.reasoning_tokens` when the top-level field is 0 — this is
  91:       BLOCKING for Mirror/Judge at xhigh reasoning (reasoning dominates their cost).
  92:     * conservative `max(api_cost, imputed)`: OpenRouter omits `usage.cost` for some models, so
  93:       the impute path is live; for a budget guard over-counting is the safe direction.
  94:     * FLOOR (I-meta-008 P1 / Codex design-review): when the computed cost is 0.0 AND every
  95:       extracted token (prompt + completion + reasoning) is zero AND there is no positive API
  96:       cost, floor at the ~500/100 shape. The prior `cost == 0.0 and not usage` only caught
  97:       None/{}; a NON-EMPTY all-zero usage block (e.g. `{"prompt_tokens": 0, ...}`) would still
  98:       record $0 and slip the cap — this token-level guard closes that hole.
  99:     """
 100:     usage_block = usage or {}
 101:     input_tokens = int(usage_block.get("prompt_tokens", 0) or 0)
 102:     output_tokens = int(usage_block.get("completion_tokens", 0) or 0)
 103:     reasoning_tokens = int(usage_block.get("reasoning_tokens", 0) or 0)
 104:     if not reasoning_tokens:
 105:         details = usage_block.get("completion_tokens_details") or {}
 106:         reasoning_tokens = int(details.get("reasoning_tokens", 0) or 0)
 107: 
 108:     imputed = _orc._impute_cost_from_tokens(
 109:         model_slug, input_tokens, output_tokens, reasoning_tokens
 110:     )
 111:     api_cost = float(usage_block.get("cost", 0) or 0)
 112:     cost = max(api_cost, imputed)
 113: 
 114:     # I-meta-008 P1 zero-usage floor: token-level, NOT block-presence. A non-empty all-zero
 115:     # usage block (or absent usage) with no positive api cost must be floored, never billed $0.
 116:     if (
 117:         cost == 0.0
 118:         and input_tokens == 0
