 129: class RecordingTransport:
 130:     """Wrap an injected `RoleTransport`; record EVERY completion before returning it.
 131: 
 132:     On each `complete(request)` the wrapper appends a `RoleCallRecord(role, model_slug,
 133:     served_model, raw_text, parsed=None)` to `self.records` BEFORE returning the underlying
 134:     response (Codex iter-2 P1-4). Because the record is appended before the adapter sees the
 135:     response — and therefore before the adapter can parse or raise — the served-identity
 136:     record survives even on the fail-closed paths (a Mirror pass-1 that then raises
 137:     `MirrorCitationError`). `parsed` is left None here: it is the role contract that parses,
 138:     and the parsed sub-results are carried separately on `ClaimPipelineResult`.

  76: def _role_pins() -> list[RolePin]:
  77:     """Build the FOUR per-role pins (generator/mirror/sentinel/judge) from the lock + env.
  78: 
  79:     I-meta-002 sub-PR-5: the 2-role (generator+evaluator) pin set is replaced by the locked
  80:     4-role set. The post-run gate enforces completeness in BOTH directions — every pinned role
  81:     must be observed AND every observed call must be pinned (pathB_run_gate.assert_post_run
  82:     lines 471/479) — so the pin set must EXACTLY match the captured roles. The 4-role pipeline
  83:     emits generator/mirror/sentinel/judge calls; a leftover legacy 'evaluator' pin would
  84:     therefore gate-FAIL at runtime (no evaluator call is captured). No production caller pins
  85:     'evaluator' directly (only this function feeds preflight via gate_around_question), so the
  86:     role is dropped here cleanly.
  87: 
  88:     Default slugs are LOCK-SOURCED via load_lock() (Codex P2, accepted) so the pins and the
  89:     architecture lock cannot drift; per-role PG_*_MODEL env vars override on top. The generator
  90:     keeps its PG_GENERATOR_MODEL > OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL > lock-default precedence.
  91: 
  92:     validate_role_families() runs on the effective 4-role map so the N-way family invariant
  93:     (all 4 lineages distinct) holds at pin-build time — a same-family misconfiguration fails
  94:     LOUD here rather than silently at runtime.
  95: 
  96:     Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P1 #2: surrogate_fields are ONLY those PROVEN present in the served
  97:     response (provider_name + model). assert_post_run treats a missing surrogate field as
  98:     fatal; system_fingerprint is recorded when present but is NOT a required surrogate.

 127: @contextlib.contextmanager
 128: def gate_around_question(
 129:     *, enabled: bool, run_dir: Path, control_vars: list[str] | None = None,
 130: ) -> Iterator[None]:
 131:     """Wrap one benchmark question's run with preflight + post-run assertion.
 132: 
 133:     Usage in the runner:
 134:         with gate_around_question(enabled=args.pathB_gate, run_dir=run_dir):
 135:             ... process_query body, including the role-tagged LLM calls ...
 136:             # On normal exit, assert_post_run runs (raises GateError if not full-power).
 137: 
 138:     Behavior:
 139:     - enabled=False: no-op (yields immediately, no capture, no preflight).
 140:     - enabled=True: preflight (raises GateError if not full-power); register_pathB_capture;
 141:       yield; on normal exit, assert_post_run; persist pin + result to ``run_dir``. On
 142:       exception inside the body, capture is cleared but the exception propagates.
 143:     """
 144:     if not enabled:
 145:         yield
 146:         return
 147: 
 148:     pin_path = run_dir / "pathB_gate_pin.json"
 149:     result_path = run_dir / "pathB_gate_result.json"
 150:     invalid_sentinel = run_dir / "pathB_gate_INVALID"
 151:     run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 152: 
 153:     # Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P3: write a FAIL result file even when preflight raises,
 154:     # so a missing-credential / unreachable-backend failure has an explicit per-run record
 155:     # (otherwise the only artifact is a stderr exception, no traceable artifact).
 156:     try:
 157:         pin = preflight(
 158:             control_vars=list(control_vars or []),
 159:             role_pins=_role_pins(),
 160:             salt=_salt(),
 161:             roots=[Path("src/polaris_graph"), Path("scripts")],
 162:             offline=False,  # real run = real reachability ping (gate enforce-by-default).
 163:         )
 164:     except GateError as exc:
 165:         result_path.write_text(
 166:             json.dumps(
 167:                 {"verdict": "FAIL", "stage": "preflight", "reason": str(exc)},
 168:                 indent=2, sort_keys=True,
 169:             ),
 170:             encoding="utf-8",
 171:         )
 172:         invalid_sentinel.write_text(
 173:             f"preflight FAIL: {exc}\n", encoding="utf-8",
 174:         )
 175:         logger.error("[pathB] preflight FAIL: %s", exc)
 176:         raise
 177:     pin_path.write_text(json.dumps(pin, indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str),
 178:                         encoding="utf-8")
 179:     _capture.register_pathB_capture()
 180:     # I-bug-946 (#932): publish the resolved per-role provider mapping via ContextVar so
 181:     # openrouter_client and entailment_judge force singleton routing in their request bodies.
 182:     # Without this, OpenRouter's silent fallback re-routes mid-run and the post_run gate fails
 183:     # (smoke #15: evaluator served by Novita while pin expected Fireworks).
 184:     role_provider_map = {
 185:         rp["role"]: rp["provider_name"]
 186:         for rp in pin.get("role_pins", [])
 187:         if rp.get("provider_name")
 188:     }
 189:     rp_token = _capture.set_role_providers(role_provider_map) if role_provider_map else None
 190:     try:
 191:         yield
 192:     except Exception:
 193:         # Propagate; do not run assert_post_run on a failed run (it would mask the cause).
 194:         if rp_token is not None:
 195:             _capture.reset_role_providers(rp_token)
 196:         _capture.clear_pathB_capture()

  99: def current_role_provider() -> str | None:
 100:     """Return the resolved provider for the CURRENT role (read via _ROLE contextvar).
 101: 
 102:     Returns None if either the gate is off (mapping is None) or the current role has no
 103:     entry in the mapping. openrouter_client calls this; when None it falls back to its
 104:     current env-driven path (gate-off mode).
 105: 
 106:     NOTE: entailment_judge must NOT use this — see get_role_provider() below.
 107:     """
 108:     mapping = _ROLE_PROVIDER.get()
 109:     if mapping is None:
 110:         return None
 111:     role = _ROLE.get()
 112:     if role is None:
 113:         return None
 114:     return mapping.get(role)
 115:

 117: def get_role_provider(role: str) -> str | None:
 118:     """Explicit-role lookup, NOT keyed off the ambient _ROLE contextvar.

 124:     silent re-route. The judge must pass role="evaluator" explicitly.
 125:     """
 126:     mapping = _ROLE_PROVIDER.get()
 127:     if mapping is None:
 128:         return None

  69: # CURRENT dev/benchmark stage (saves GPU cost). "self_host" selects the lock's sovereign route.
  70: _FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT_ENV = "PG_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT"
  71: _TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER = "openrouter"
  72: _TRANSPORT_SELF_HOST = "self_host"
  73: _FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT_DEFAULT = _TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER
  74: 
  75: # OpenRouter catalog endpoint (GET) for the benchmark-stage slug-resolution preflight.
  76: _OPENROUTER_MODELS_PATH = "/models"
  77: 
  78: # httpx client timeout knob (LAW VI). I-meta-008 FULL-POWER: use the generous verifier timeout
  79: # (default 900s) so the client default never undercuts the reasoning verifiers' per-request budget.
  80: _TIMEOUT_SECONDS = int(os.getenv("PG_VERIFIER_LLM_TIMEOUT_SECONDS", "900"))
  81: 
  82: 
  83: def four_role_transport_mode() -> str:
  84:     """Resolve `PG_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT` (I-meta-007d). DEFAULT "openrouter" at the dev/benchmark
  85:     stage (saves GPU cost; OpenRouter is a US router — dev/benchmark ONLY, never the sovereign
  86:     demo). "self_host" selects the lock's `vast_self_host*` route. Fails loud on an unknown value
  87:     so a typo never silently picks the wrong (spend) route.
  88:     """
  89:     mode = os.getenv(_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT_ENV, _FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT_DEFAULT).strip().lower()
  90:     if mode not in (_TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER, _TRANSPORT_SELF_HOST):
  91:         raise ValueError(
  92:             f"{_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT_ENV}={mode!r} is invalid; expected "
  93:             f"{_TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER!r} (benchmark-stage OpenRouter, default) or "
  94:             f"{_TRANSPORT_SELF_HOST!r} (lock sovereign self-host route)."
  95:         )
  96:     return mode
  97: 
  98: 
  99: def build_gate_b_transport(
 100:     http_client: httpx.Client | None = None,
 101: ) -> OpenRouterRoleTransport | OpenAICompatibleRoleTransport:
 102:     """Construct the verifier transport (one shared sync `httpx.Client`), ENV-GATED per
 103:     `PG_FOUR_ROLE_TRANSPORT` (I-meta-007d).
 104: 
 105:     Built INSIDE this function (never at module level) so importing `run_gate_b` opens no
 106:     client and touches no socket.
 107: 
 108:     - "openrouter" (DEFAULT, dev/benchmark stage — saves GPU cost): returns an
 109:       `OpenRouterRoleTransport` that, when invoked, POSTs `/chat/completions` to OpenRouter with
 110:       each role's lock-pinned slug AND MAX reasoning. SOVEREIGNTY: OpenRouter is a US router —
 111:       acceptable for dev/benchmark ONLY; the lock's `vast_self_host*` self-host route remains
 112:       the FINAL SOVEREIGN destination (the lock is NOT mutated).
 113:     - "self_host": returns the original `OpenAICompatibleRoleTransport` (per-role
 114:       `PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL` self-hosted vLLM) — the lock's sovereign serving route.
 115: 
 116:     `http_client` (P2): the live caller passes nothing, so a real `httpx.Client` is built here;
 117:     tests inject a `MockTransport`-backed client so transport-selection is exercised with no live
 118:     client and no socket. Resolved ONCE and handed to whichever transport is selected.
 119: 
 120:     The live invocation is the later operator-authorized Gate-B canary, never a test.
 121:     """
 122:     client = http_client if http_client is not None else httpx.Client(timeout=_TIMEOUT_SECONDS)
 123:     if four_role_transport_mode() == _TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER:
 124:         return OpenRouterRoleTransport(client)
 125:     return OpenAICompatibleRoleTransport(client)
 126: 
 127: 
 128: def verifier_model_slugs() -> dict[str, str]:
 129:     """Return the pinned `{mirror,sentinel,judge: model_slug}` map for the ACTIVE transport mode.
 130: 
 131:     MODE-AWARE (I-meta-007d P1-1) so served == pinned on whichever route is active:
 132:       - "openrouter" (benchmark, DEFAULT): the BENCHMARK lineup
 133:         (`benchmark_verifier_lineup` — the operator-chosen OpenRouter slugs in
 134:         role_selection_final.md: Mirror `z-ai/glm-5.1`, Sentinel `ibm-granite/granite-4.1-8b`,
 135:         Judge `qwen/qwen3.6-35b-a3b`). The transport POSTs these exact slugs as `body["model"]`,
 136:         so the pin the builder threads into `RoleRequest.model_slug` matches the served slug.
 137:       - "self_host": the lock's self-host `model_slug`s (Mirror `cohere/command-a-plus`,
 138:         Sentinel the granite-GUARDIAN, Judge `qwen/qwen3.6-35b-a3b`) — the sovereign serving
 139:         route, served by `OpenAICompatibleRoleTransport` against `PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL`.
 140: 
 141:     The single machine-readable source of truth per mode (LAW VI). The generator slug is
 142:     intentionally excluded — it is not a per-claim verifier role.
 143:     """
 144:     if four_role_transport_mode() == _TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER:
 145:         return benchmark_verifier_lineup()
 146:     lock = load_lock()
 147:     return {role: lock["required_roles"][role]["model_slug"] for role in _VERIFIER_ROLES}
 148: 
 149: 
 150: def make_gate_b_input_builder(
 151:     *,
 152:     d8_config_path: str | Path | None = None,
 153: ) -> Callable[..., NativeGateBBundle]:
 154:     """Return the Gate-B builder CLOSURE — a factory over RESOLUTION POLICY only.
 155: 
 156:     The closure captures ONLY the resolution policy (the optional `d8_config_path` + the
 157:     normalization fn + the lock-slug source) — NOT the run-local report objects, which do not
 158:     exist when the caller constructs the builder (they are produced inside `run_one_query` after
 159:     generation). The SEAM calls the closure AFTER generation, passing the run-local objects
 160:     (`multi`, `template`, `slug`, `domain`, `ev_pool`) as keyword args. The closure then OWNS
 161:     resolution: it normalizes the run's raw `ev_pool` into the builder's
 162:     `{evidence_id: {text, doi?, pmid?, url?}}` record contract (deterministic, no network — keys
 163:     preserve the ProvenanceToken.evidence_id space), loads the D8 policy config, sources the
 164:     pinned verifier slugs from the lock, and calls the native `build_native_gate_b_inputs`.
 165:     NATIVE-ONLY: nothing here reads the gold rubric.
 166:     """
 167: 
 168:     def _builder(
 169:         *,
 170:         multi: Any,
 171:         template: dict,
 172:         slug: str,
 173:         domain: str,
 174:         ev_pool: Mapping[str, Mapping[str, Any]],
 175:     ) -> NativeGateBBundle:
 176:         evidence_lookup = normalize_evidence_pool_lookup(ev_pool)
 177:         d8_config = load_d8_policy_config(d8_config_path)
 178:         model_slugs = verifier_model_slugs()
 179:         return build_native_gate_b_inputs(
 180:             multi=multi,
 181:             template=template,
 182:             slug=slug,
 183:             domain=domain,
 184:             evidence_lookup=evidence_lookup,
 185:             model_slugs=model_slugs,
 186:             d8_config=d8_config,
 187:         )
 188: 
 189:     return _builder
 190: 
 191: 
 192: def enable_four_role_mode() -> None:
 193:     """Set `PG_FOUR_ROLE_MODE=1` in the process env so the guarded sweep branch activates.
 194: 
 195:     Wiring helper (LAW VI: env-driven activation). The Gate-B live run sets this before
 196:     invoking the sweep; the offline seam test sets it via monkeypatch instead.
 197:     """
 198:     os.environ[_FOUR_ROLE_MODE_ENV] = "1"
 199: 
 200: 
 201: def assert_four_role_families_distinct() -> dict[str, str]:
 202:     """Assert the 4 roles (generator + the 3 verifiers) are all DISTINCT lineages for the
 203:     ACTIVE transport mode (the N-way two-family invariant, CLAUDE.md §9.1 / family_policy:
 204:     all_distinct). Fails LOUD (I-meta-007) — a collision would let one family self-verify.
 205:     Returns the `{role: family}` map for telemetry.
 206: 
 207:     MODE-AWARE (I-meta-007d P1-1): the family check must run over the families ACTUALLY served:
 208:       - "openrouter" (benchmark, DEFAULT): generator family from the lock (`deepseek` — the
 209:         generator is unchanged + runs upstream on OpenRouter) UNION the 3 BENCHMARK verifier
 210:         families (`benchmark_verifier_family`: Mirror `z-ai`, Sentinel `ibm-granite`, Judge
 211:         `qwen`). These four — deepseek / z-ai / ibm-granite / qwen — are distinct. (Checking the
 212:         LOCK's verifier families here would assert on `cohere`/`ibm-granite`/`qwen`, which are NOT
 213:         the families served on this route.)
 214:       - "self_host": the lock's families for all 4 roles (the sovereign route).
 215:     """
 216:     lock = load_lock()
 217:     if four_role_transport_mode() == _TRANSPORT_OPENROUTER:
 218:         fams = {"generator": str(lock["required_roles"]["generator"]["family"])}
 219:         for role in _VERIFIER_ROLES:
 220:             fams[role] = benchmark_verifier_family(role)
